err\n   167→\t\t}\n   168→\n   169→\t\tfor _, doc := range docs {\n   170→\t\t\tif err := fn(doc); err != nil {\n   171→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   172→\t\t\t}\n   173→\t\t}\n   174→\t}\n   175→\n   176→\treturn nil\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→// documentsFromFile parses and validates a document from a single fs.File instance\n   180→func documentsFromFile(fi fs.File, opts SnapshotOption) ([]*ext.Document, error) {\n   181→\tvalidator, err := validation.NewFeaturesValidator(opts.validatorOption...)\n   182→\tif err != nil {\n   183→\t\treturn nil, err\n   184→\t}\n   185→\n   186→\tstat, err := fi.Stat()\n   187→\tif err != nil {\n   188→\t\treturn nil, err\n   189→\t}\n   190→\n   191→\tbuf := &bytes.Buffer{}\n   192→\treader := io.TeeReader(fi, buf)\n   193→\n   194→\tvar docs []*ext.Document\n   195→\textn := filepath.Ext(stat.Name())\n   196→\n   197→\tvar decode func(any) error\n   198→\tswitch extn {\n   199→\tcase \".yaml\", \".yml\":\n   200→\t\t// Support YAML stream by looping until we reach an EOF.\n   201→\t\tdecode = yaml.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n   202→\tcase \"\", \".json\":\n   203→\t\tdecode = json.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n   204→\tdefault:\n   205→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected extension: %q\", extn)\n   206→\t}\n   207→\n   208→\t// validate after we have checked supported\n   209→\t// extensions but before we attempt to decode the\n   210→\t// buffers contents to ensure we fill the buffer\n   211→\t// via the TeeReader\n   212→\tif err := validator.Validate(stat.Name(), reader); err != nil {\n   213→\t\treturn nil, err\n   214→\t}\n   215→\n   216→\tfor {\n   217→\t\tdoc := &ext.Document{}\n   218→\t\tif err := decode(doc); err != nil {\n   219→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n   220→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   221→\t\t\t}\n   222→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   223→\t\t}\n   224→\n   225→\t\t// set namespace to default if empty in document\n   226→\t\tif doc.Namespace == \"\" {\n   227→\t\t\tdoc.Namespace = \"default\"\n   228→\t\t}\n   229→\t\tdocs = append(docs, doc)\n   230→\t}\n   231→\n   232→\treturn docs, nil\n   233→}\n   234→\n   235→// listStateFiles lists all the file paths in a provided fs.FS containing Flipt feature state\n   236→func listStateFiles(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS) ([]string, error) {\n   237→\tidx, err := OpenFliptIndex(logger, src)\n   238→\tif err != nil {\n   239→\t\treturn nil, err\n   240→\t}\n   241→\n   242→\tvar paths []string\n   243→\tif err := fs.WalkDir(src, \".\", func(path string, d fs.DirEntry, err error) error {\n   244→\t\tif err != nil {\n   245→\t\t\treturn err\n   246→\t\t}\n   247→\n   248→\t\tif d.IsDir() {\n   249→\t\t\treturn nil\n   250→\t\t}\n   251→\n   252→\t\tif idx.Match(path) {\n   253→\t\t\tpaths = append(paths, path)\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\n   256→\t\treturn nil\n   257→\t}); err != nil {\n   258→\t\treturn nil, err\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\treturn paths, nil\n   262→}\n   263→\n   264→func (ss *Snapshot) addDoc(doc *ext.Document) error {\n   265→\tns := ss.ns[doc.Namespace]\n   266→\tif ns == nil {\n   267→\t\tns = newNamespace(doc.Namespace, doc.Namespace, ss.now)\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\tevalDists := map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}\n   271→\tif len(ss.evalDists) > 0 {\n   272→\t\tevalDists = ss.evalDists\n   273→\t}\n   274→\n   275→\tfor _, s := range doc.Segments {\n   276→\t\tmatchType := flipt.MatchType_value[s.MatchType]\n   277→\t\tsegment := &flipt.Segment{\n   278→\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   279→\t\t\tName:         s.Name,\n   280→\t\t\tKey:          s.Key,\n   281→\t\t\tDescription:  s.Description,\n   282→\t\t\tMatchType:    flipt.MatchType(matchType),\n   283→\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   284→\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   285→\t\t}\n   286→\n   287→\t\tfor _, constraint := range s.Constraints {\n   288→\t\t\tconstraintType := flipt.ComparisonType_value[constraint.Type]\n   289→\t\t\tsegment.Constraints = append(segment.Constraints, &flipt.Constraint{\n   290→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   291→\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:   segment.Key,\n   292→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   293→\t\t\t\tOperator:     constraint.Operator,\n   294→\t\t\t\tProperty:     constraint.Property,\n   295→\t\t\t\tType:         flipt.ComparisonType(constraintType),\n   296→\t\t\t\tValue:        constraint.Value,\n   297→\t\t\t\tDescription:  constraint.Description,\n   298→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   299→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   300→\t\t\t})\n   301→\t\t}\n   302→\n   303→\t\tns.segments[segment.Key] = segment\n   304→\t}\n   305→\n   306→\tfor _, f := range doc.Flags {\n   307→\t\tflagType := flipt.FlagType_value[f.Type]\n   308→\t\tflag := &flipt.Flag{\n   309→\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   310→\t\t\tKey:          f.Key,\n   311→\t\t\tName:         f.Name,\n   312→\t\t\tDescription:  f.Description,\n   313→\t\t\tEnabled:      f.Enabled,\n   314→\t\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType(flagType),\n   315→\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   316→\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   317→\t\t}\n   318→\n   319→\t\tfor _, v := range f.Variants {\n   320→\t\t\tattachment, err := json.Marshal(v.Attachment)\n   321→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   322→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   323→\t\t\t}\n   324→\n   325→\t\t\tflag.Variants = append(flag.Variants, &flipt.Variant{\n   326→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   327→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   328→\t\t\t\tKey:          v.Key,\n   329→\t\t\t\tName:         v.Name,\n   330→\t\t\t\tDescription:  v.Description,\n   331→\t\t\t\tAttachment:   string(attachment),\n   332→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   333→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   334→\t\t\t})\n   335→\t\t}\n   336→\n   337→\t\tns.flags[f.Key] = flag\n   338→\n   339→\t\tevalRules := []*storage.EvaluationRule{}\n   340→\t\tfor i, r := range f.Rules {\n   341→\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n   342→\t\t\trule := &flipt.Rule{\n   343→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   344→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   345→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   346→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   347→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   348→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   349→\t\t\t}\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\tevalRule := &storage.EvaluationRule{\n   352→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   353→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   354→\t\t\t\tID:           rule.Id,\n   355→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   356→\t\t\t}\n   357→\n   358→\t\t\tswitch s := r.Segment.IsSegment.(type) {\n   359→\t\t\tcase ext.SegmentKey:\n   360→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKey = string(s)\n   361→\t\t\tcase *ext.Segments:\n   362→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKeys = s.Keys\n   363→\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[s.SegmentOperator]\n   364→\n   365→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator)\n   366→\t\t\t}\n   367→\n   368→\t\t\tvar (\n   369→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n   370→\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n   371→\t\t\t)\n   372→\n   373→\t\t\tif rule.SegmentKey != \"\" {\n   374→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKey)\n   375→\t\t\t} else if len(rule.SegmentKeys) > 0 {\n   376→\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKeys...)\n   377→\t\t\t}\n   378→\n   379→\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n   380→\t\t\t\tsegment := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n   381→\t\t\t\tif segment == nil {\n   382→\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n   383→\t\t\t\t}\n   384→\n   385→\t\t\t\tevc := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n   386→\t\t\t\tfor _, constraint := range segment.Constraints {\n   387→\t\t\t\t\tevc = append(evc, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n   388→\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: constraint.Operator,\n   389→\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: constraint.Property,\n   390→\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     constraint.Type,\n   391→\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    constraint.Value,\n   392→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   393→\t\t\t\t}\n   394→\n   395→\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n   396→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n   397→\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n   398→\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: evc,\n   399→\t\t\t\t}\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\n   402→\t\t\tif rule.SegmentOperator == flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR {\n   403→\t\t\t\tevalRule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n   404→\t\t\t}\n   405→\n   406→\t\t\tevalRule.Segments = segments\n   407→\n   408→\t\t\tevalRules = append(evalRules, evalRule)\n   409→\n   410→\t\t\tfor _, d := range r.Distributions {\n   411→\t\t\t\tvariant, found := findByKey(d.VariantKey, flag.Variants...)\n   412→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   413→\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown variant %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, d.VariantKey)\n   414→\t\t\t\t}\n   415→\n   416→\t\t\t\tid := uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String()\n   417→\t\t\t\trule.Distributions = append(rule.Distributions, &flipt.Distribution{\n   418→\t\t\t\t\tId:        id,\n   419→\t\t\t\t\tRollout:   d.Rollout,\n   420→\t\t\t\t\tRuleId:    rule.Id,\n   421→\t\t\t\t\tVariantId: variant.Id,\n   422→\t\t\t\t\tCreatedAt: ss.now,\n   423→\t\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt: ss.now,\n   424→\t\t\t\t})\n   425→\n   426→\t\t\t\tevalDists[evalRule.ID] = append(evalDists[evalRule.ID], &storage.EvaluationDistribution{\n   427→\t\t\t\t\tID:                id,\n   428→\t\t\t\t\tRollout:           d.Rollout,\n   429→\t\t\t\t\tVariantID:         variant.Id,\n   430→\t\t\t\t\tVariantKey:        variant.Key,\n   431→\t\t\t\t\tVariantAttachment: variant.Attachment,\n   432→\t\t\t\t})\n   433→\t\t\t}\n   434→\n   435→\t\t\tns.rules[rule.Id] = rule\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\n   438→\t\tns.evalRules[f.Key] = evalRules\n   439→\n   440→\t\tevalRollouts := make([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, 0, len(f.Rollouts))\n   441→\t\tfor i, rollout := range f.Rollouts {\n   442→\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n   443→\t\t\ts := &storage.EvaluationRollout{\n   444→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   445→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   446→\t\t\t}\n   447→\n   448→\t\t\tflagRollout := &flipt.Rollout{\n   449→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   450→\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n   451→\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n   452→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   453→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   454→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   455→\t\t\t}\n   456→\n   457→\t\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n   458→\t\t\t\ts.Threshold = &storage.RolloutThreshold{\n   459→\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n   460→\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n   461→\t\t\t\t}\n   462→\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_THRESHOLD_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n   463→\n   464→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n   465→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Threshold{\n   466→\t\t\t\t\tThreshold: &flipt.RolloutThreshold{\n   467→\t\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n   468→\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n   469→\t\t\t\t\t},\n   470→\t\t\t\t}\n   471→\t\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n   472→\t\t\t\tvar (\n   473→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n   474→\t\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n   475→\t\t\t\t)\n   476→\n   477→\t\t\t\tif rollout.Segment.Key != \"\" {\n   478→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Key)\n   479→\t\t\t\t} else if len(rollout.Segment.Keys) > 0 {\n   480→\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Keys...)\n   481→\t\t\t\t}\n   482→\n   483→\t\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n   484→\t\t\t\t\tsegment, ok := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n   485→\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   486→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n   487→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   488→\n   489→\t\t\t\t\tconstraints := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n   490→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, c := range segment.Constraints {\n   491→\t\t\t\t\t\tconstraints = append(constraints, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n   492→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: c.Operator,\n   493→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: c.Property,\n   494→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     c.Type,\n   495→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    c.Value,\n   496→\t\t\t\t\t\t})\n   497→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   498→\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n   501→\t\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n   502→\t\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: constraints,\n   503→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   504→\t\t\t\t}\n   505→\n   506→\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[rollout.Segment.Operator]\n   507→\n   508→\t\t\t\ts.Segment = &storage.RolloutSegment{\n   509→\t\t\t\t\tSegments:        segments,\n   510→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n   512→\t\t\t\t}\n   513→\n   514→\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_SEGMENT_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n   515→\n   516→\t\t\t\tfrs := &flipt.RolloutSegment{\n   517→\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n   519→\t\t\t\t}\n   520→\n   521→\t\t\t\tif len(segmentKeys) == 1 {\n   522→\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKey = segmentKeys[0]\n   523→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   524→\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n   525→\t\t\t\t}\n   526→\n   527→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n   528→\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Segment{\n   529→\t\t\t\t\tSegment: frs,\n   530→\t\t\t\t}\n   531→\t\t\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t\t\tns.rollouts[flagRollout.Id] = flagRollout\n   534→\n   535→\t\t\tevalRollouts = append(evalRollouts, s)\n   536→\t\t}\n   537→\n   538→\t\tns.evalRollouts[f.Key] = evalRollouts\n   539→\t}\n   540→\n   541→\tss.ns[doc.Namespace] = ns\n   542→\n   543→\tss.evalDists = evalDists\n   544→\n   545→\treturn nil\n   546→}\n   547→\n   548→func (ss Snapshot) String() string {\n   549→\treturn \"snapshot\"\n   550→}\n   551→\n   552→func (ss *Snapshot) GetRule(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest, id string) (rule *flipt.Rule, _ error) {\n   553→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n   554→\tif err != nil {\n   555→\t\treturn nil, err\n   556→\t}\n   557→\n   558→\tvar ok bool\n   559→\trule, ok = ns.rules[id]\n   560→\tif !ok {\n   561→\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(`rule \"%s/%s\"`, p.Namespace(), id)\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\treturn rule, nil\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→func (ss *Snapshot) ListRules(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ResourceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Rule], _ error) {\n   568→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n   569→\tif err != nil {\n   570→\t\treturn set, err\n   571→\t}\n   572→\n   573→\trules := make([]*flipt.Rule, 0, len(ns.rules))\n   574→\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n   575→\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Predicate.Key {\n   576→\t\t\trules = append(rules, rule)\n   577→\t\t}\n   578→\t}\n   579→\n   580→\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n   581→\t\treturn rules[i].Rank < rules[j].Rank\n   582→\t}, rules...)\n   583→}\n   584→\n   585→func (ss *Snapshot) CountRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n   586→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n   587→\tif err != nil {\n   588→\t\treturn 0, err\n   589→\t}\n   590→\n   591→\tvar count uint64 = 0\n   592→\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n   593→\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Key {\n   594→\t\t\tcount += 1\n   595→\t\t}\n   596→\t}\n   597→\n   598→\treturn count, nil\n   599→}\n   600→\n   601→func (ss *Snapshot) GetSegment(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Segment, error) {\n   602→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n   603→\tif err != nil {\n   604→\t\treturn nil, err\n   605→\t}\n   606→\n   607→\tsegment, ok := ns.segments[req.Key]\n   608→\tif !ok {\n   609→\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(\"segment %q\", req)\n   610→\t}\n   611→\n   612→\treturn segment, nil\n   613→}\n   614→\n   615→func (ss *Snapshot) ListSegments(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.NamespaceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Segment], err error) {\n   616→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n   617→\tif err != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn set, err\n   619→\t}\n   620→\n   621→\tsegments := make([]*flipt.Segment, 0, len(ns.segments))\n   622→\tfor _, segment := range ns.segments {\n   623→\t\tsegments = append(segments, segment)\n   624→\t}\n   625→\n   626→\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n   627→\t\treturn segments[i].Key < segments[j].Key\n   628→\t}, segments...)\n   629→}\n   630→\n   631→func (ss *Snapshot) CountSegments(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n   632→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n   633→\tif err != nil {\n   634→\t\treturn 0, err\n   635→\t}\n   636→\n   637→\treturn uint64(len(ns.segments)), nil\n   638→}\n   639→\n   640→func (ss *Snapshot) GetNamespace(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (*flipt.Namespace, error) {\n   641→\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n   642→\tif err != nil {\n   643→\t\treturn nil, err\n   644→\t}\n   645→\n   646→\treturn ns.resource, nil\n   647→}\n   648→\n   649→func (ss *Snapshot) ListNamespaces(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ReferenceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Namespace], err error) {\n   650→\tns := make([]*flipt.Namespace, 0, len(ss.ns))\n   651→\tfor _, n := range ss.ns {\n   652→\t\tns = append(ns, n.resource)\n   653→\t}\n   654→\n   655→\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n   656→\t\treturn ns[i].Key < ns[j].Key\n   657→\t}, ns...)\n   658→}\n 840→\tend := offset + int(params.Limit)\n   841→\tif end > len(set.Results) {\n   842→\t\tend = len(set.Results)\n   843→\t} else if end < len(set.Results) {\n   844→\t\t// set next page token given EOF.\n\t\tdecode = yaml.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n\tcase \"\", \".json\":\n\t\tdecode = json.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected extension: %q\", extn)\n\t}\n\n\t// validate after we have checked supported\n\t// extensions but before we attempt to decode the\n\t// buffers contents to ensure we fill the buffer\n\t// via the TeeReader\n\tif err := validator.Validate(stat.Name(), reader); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tdoc := &ext.Document{}\n\t\tif err := decode(doc); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// set namespace to default if empty in document\n\t\tif doc.Namespace == \"\" {\n\t\t\tdoc.Namespace = \"default\"\n\t\t}\n\t\tdocs = append(docs, doc)\n\t}\n\n\treturn docs, nil\n}\n\n// listStateFiles lists all the file paths in a provided fs.FS containing Flipt feature state\nfunc listStateFiles(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS) ([]string, error) {\n\tidx, err := OpenFliptIndex(logger, src)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar paths []string\n\tif err := fs.WalkDir(src, \".\", func(path string, d fs.DirEntry, err error) error {\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif d.IsDir() {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif idx.Match(path) {\n\t\t\tpaths = append(paths, path)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn paths, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) addDoc(doc *ext.Document) error {\n\tns := ss.ns[doc.Namespace]\n\tif ns == nil {\n\t\tns = newNamespace(doc.Namespace, doc.Namespace, ss.now)\n\t}\n\n\tevalDists := map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}\n\tif len(ss.evalDists) > 0 {\n\t\tevalDists = ss.evalDists\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, s := range doc.Segments {\n\t\tmatchType := flipt.MatchType_value[s.MatchType]\n\t\tsegment := &flipt.Segment{\n\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\tName:         s.Name,\n\t\t\tKey:          s.Key,\n\t\t\tDescription:  s.Description,\n\t\t\tMatchType:    flipt.MatchType(matchType),\n\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, constraint := range s.Constraints {\n\t\t\tconstraintType := flipt.ComparisonType_value[constraint.Type]\n\t\t\tsegment.Constraints = append(segment.Constraints, &flipt.Constraint{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:   segment.Key,\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tOperator:     constraint.Operator,\n\t\t\t\tProperty:     constraint.Property,\n\t\t\t\tType:         flipt.ComparisonType(constraintType),\n\t\t\t\tValue:        constraint.Value,\n\t\t\t\tDescription:  constraint.Description,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.segments[segment.Key] = segment\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, f := range doc.Flags {\n\t\tflagType := flipt.FlagType_value[f.Type]\n\t\tflag := &flipt.Flag{\n\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\tKey:          f.Key,\n\t\t\tName:         f.Name,\n\t\t\tDescription:  f.Description,\n\t\t\tEnabled:      f.Enabled,\n\t\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType(flagType),\n\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, v := range f.Variants {\n\t\t\tattachment, err := json.Marshal(v.Attachment)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tflag.Variants = append(flag.Variants, &flipt.Variant{\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tKey:          v.Key,\n\t\t\t\tName:         v.Name,\n\t\t\t\tDescription:  v.Description,\n\t\t\t\tAttachment:   string(attachment),\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.flags[f.Key] = flag\n\n\t\tevalRules := []*storage.EvaluationRule{}\n\t\tfor i, r := range f.Rules {\n\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n\t\t\trule := &flipt.Rule{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevalRule := &storage.EvaluationRule{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tID:           rule.Id,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tswitch s := r.Segment.IsSegment.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase ext.SegmentKey:\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKey = string(s)\n\t\t\tcase *ext.Segments:\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKeys = s.Keys\n\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[s.SegmentOperator]\n\n\t\t\t\trule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tif rule.SegmentKey != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKey)\n\t\t\t} else if len(rule.SegmentKeys) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rule.SegmentKeys...)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n\t\t\t\tsegment := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n\t\t\t\tif segment == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tevc := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n\t\t\t\tfor _, constraint := range segment.Constraints {\n\t\t\t\t\tevc = append(evc, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: constraint.Operator,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: constraint.Property,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     constraint.Type,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    constraint.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: evc,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif rule.SegmentOperator == flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR {\n\t\t\t\tevalRule.SegmentOperator = flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevalRule.Segments = segments\n\n\t\t\tevalRules = append(evalRules, evalRule)\n\n\t\t\tfor _, d := range r.Distributions {\n\t\t\t\tvariant, found := findByKey(d.VariantKey, flag.Variants...)\n\t\t\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown variant %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, d.VariantKey)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tid := uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String()\n\t\t\t\trule.Distributions = append(rule.Distributions, &flipt.Distribution{\n\t\t\t\t\tId:        id,\n\t\t\t\t\tRollout:   d.Rollout,\n\t\t\t\t\tRuleId:    rule.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantId: variant.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tCreatedAt: ss.now,\n\t\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt: ss.now,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\n\t\t\t\tevalDists[evalRule.ID] = append(evalDists[evalRule.ID], &storage.EvaluationDistribution{\n\t\t\t\t\tID:                id,\n\t\t\t\t\tRollout:           d.Rollout,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantID:         variant.Id,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantKey:        variant.Key,\n\t\t\t\t\tVariantAttachment: variant.Attachment,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tns.rules[rule.Id] = rule\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.evalRules[f.Key] = evalRules\n\n\t\tevalRollouts := make([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, 0, len(f.Rollouts))\n\t\tfor i, rollout := range f.Rollouts {\n\t\t\trank := int32(i + 1)\n\t\t\ts := &storage.EvaluationRollout{\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tflagRollout := &flipt.Rollout{\n\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n\t\t\t\tRank:         rank,\n\t\t\t\tFlagKey:      f.Key,\n\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif rollout.Threshold != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.Threshold = &storage.RolloutThreshold{\n\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_THRESHOLD_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Threshold{\n\t\t\t\t\tThreshold: &flipt.RolloutThreshold{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tPercentage: rollout.Threshold.Percentage,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:      rollout.Threshold.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} else if rollout.Segment != nil {\n\t\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = []string{}\n\t\t\t\t\tsegments    = make(map[string]*storage.EvaluationSegment)\n\t\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\t\tif rollout.Segment.Key != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Key)\n\t\t\t\t} else if len(rollout.Segment.Keys) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegmentKeys = append(segmentKeys, rollout.Segment.Keys...)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tfor _, segmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n\t\t\t\t\tsegment, ok := ns.segments[segmentKey]\n\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\treturn errs.ErrInvalidf(\"flag %s/%s rule %d references unknown segment %q\", doc.Namespace, flag.Key, rank, segmentKey)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tconstraints := make([]storage.EvaluationConstraint, 0, len(segment.Constraints))\n\t\t\t\t\tfor _, c := range segment.Constraints {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tconstraints = append(constraints, storage.EvaluationConstraint{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tOperator: c.Operator,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tProperty: c.Property,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tType:     c.Type,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tValue:    c.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tsegments[segmentKey] = &storage.EvaluationSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:  segmentKey,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tMatchType:   segment.MatchType,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tConstraints: constraints,\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tsegmentOperator := flipt.SegmentOperator_value[rollout.Segment.Operator]\n\n\t\t\t\ts.Segment = &storage.RolloutSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegments:        segments,\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\ts.RolloutType = flipt.RolloutType_SEGMENT_ROLLOUT_TYPE\n\n\t\t\t\tfrs := &flipt.RolloutSegment{\n\t\t\t\t\tValue:           rollout.Segment.Value,\n\t\t\t\t\tSegmentOperator: flipt.SegmentOperator(segmentOperator),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif len(segmentKeys) == 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKey = segmentKeys[0]\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tfrs.SegmentKeys = segmentKeys\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Type = s.RolloutType\n\t\t\t\tflagRollout.Rule = &flipt.Rollout_Segment{\n\t\t\t\t\tSegment: frs,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tns.rollouts[flagRollout.Id] = flagRollout\n\n\t\t\tevalRollouts = append(evalRollouts, s)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tns.evalRollouts[f.Key] = evalRollouts\n\t}\n\n\tss.ns[doc.Namespace] = ns\n\n\tss.evalDists = evalDists\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss Snapshot) String() string {\n\treturn \"snapshot\"\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) GetRule(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest, id string) (rule *flipt.Rule, _ error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar ok bool\n\trule, ok = ns.rules[id]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf(`rule \"%s/%s\"`, p.Namespace(), id)\n\t}\n\n\treturn rule, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) ListRules(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ResourceRequest]) (set storage.ResultSet[*flipt.Rule], _ error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn set, err\n\t}\n\n\trules := make([]*flipt.Rule, 0, len(ns.rules))\n\tfor _, rule := range ns.rules {\n\t\tif rule.FlagKey == req.Predicate.Key {\n\t\t\trules = append(rules, rule)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn paginate(req.QueryParams, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn rules[i].Rank < rules[j].Rank\n\t}, rules...)\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) CountRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) {\n\t\t\tcount += 1\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn count, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) GetSegment(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Segment, error) {\n\tns, err := {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Predicate.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn set, err\n\t}\n\n\tsegments := make([]*flipt.Segment, 0, len(ns.segments))\n\tfor _, segment := range *Snapshot) CountSegments(ctx context.Context, p storage.NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(p.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn ns.resource, nil\n}\n\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) ListNamespaces(ctx context.Context, req *storage.ListRequest[storage.ReferenceRequest]) (set GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error) {\n\tns, ok := ss.ns[flag.Namespace()]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (uint64, error) {\n\tns, err := ss.getNamespace(flag.Namespace())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar count uint64 = 0\n\tfor _, rollout := range ns.rollouts {\n\t\tif rollout.FlagKey == flag.Key {\n\t\t\tcount += 1\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn count, nil\n}\n\nfunc findByKey[T interface{ GetKey() string }](key string, ts ...T) (t T, _ bool) {\n\treturn find(func(t T) bool { return t.GetKey() == key }, ts...)\n}\n\nfunc find[T any](match func(T) bool, ts ...T) (t T, _ bool) {\n\tfor _, t := range ts {\n\t\tif match(t) {\n\t\t\treturn t, true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn t, false\n}\n\nfunc paginate[T any](params storage.QueryParams, less func(i, j int) bool, items ...T) (storage.ResultSet[T], error) {\n\tif len(items) == 0 {\n\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tset := storage.ResultSet[T]{\n\t\tResults: items,\n\t}\n\n\t// sort by created_at and specified order\n\tsort.Slice(set.Results, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\tif params.Order != storage.OrderAsc {\n\t\t\ti, j = j, i\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn less(i, j)\n\t})\n\n\t// parse page token as an offset integer\n\tvar offset int\n\tv, err := strconv.ParseInt(params.PageToken, 10, 64)\n\tif params.PageToken != \"\" && err != nil {\n\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"pageToken is not valid: %q\", params.PageToken)\n\t}\n\n\toffset = int(v)\n\n\tif offset >= len(set.Results) {\n\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"invalid offset: %d\", offset)\n\t}\n\n\t// 0 means no limit on page size (all items from offset)\n\tif params.Limit == 0 {\n\t\tset.Results = set.Results[offset:]\n\t\treturn set, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// ensure end of page does not exceed entire set\n\tend := offset +
